ze/KAZEConfig.h;C:/lib/opencv2/modules/features2d/src/kaze/KAZEFeatures.h;C:/lib/opencv2/modules/features2d/src/kaze/TEvolution.h;C:/lib/opencv2/modules/features2d/src/kaze/fed.h;C:/lib/opencv2/modules/features2d/src/kaze/nldiffusion_functions.h;C:/lib/opencv2/modules/features2d/src/kaze/utils.h;C:/lib/opencv2/modules/features2d/src/precomp.hpp;$<TARGET_OBJECTS:opencv_features2d_AVX2>

PTHREAD_C_CXX_TEST_SOURCE=#include <pthread.h>

void* test_func(void* data)
{
  return data;
}

int main(void)
{
  pthread_t thread;
  pthread_create(&thread, NULL, test_func, NULL);
  pthread_detach(thread);
  pthread_join(thread, NULL);
  pthread_atfork(NULL, NULL, NULL);
  pthread_exit(NULL);

  return 0;
}
